CALLABLE FUNCTIONS, BY PURPOSE

-- Setup / lookup --
  get_latest_run_id(report_date)
      find the active run_id for a date, without copy-pasting from logs
  get_active_manifest_row(report_date)
      full manifest row (run_id, file_name, uploaded_at) for a date

-- Stage 1 — bronze --
  (use the Upload widget above)
      upload a PDF; handles new/replace/append automatically
  resolve_upload_conflict(mode)
      widget-free bypass for Replace/Append/Cancel if the buttons don't render — mode='replace'/'append'/'cancel'
  run_extraction_pipeline(run_id, report_date, pdf_bytes, file_name)
      manual Stage 1 call, if not using the widget
  reset_tables()
      DESTRUCTIVE — drops bronze + manifest entirely, not scoped to one date

-- Diagnostics --
  show_bronze_state()
      page_type counts per run_id/report_date, across everything uploaded
  dump_all_pages(pdf_bytes=None)
      full reconstructed text for every page in a PDF, with strategy labels
  dump_bronze_pages(run_id=None, report_date=None)
      same, but from stored bronze — no PDF/upload needed, works any time
  inspect_page(page_number, method='columns')
      full text for one page — compare method='columns' vs 'rows'
  debug_amount_mismatches(run_id, page_number, table_id=None)
      why specific rows failed the guard, with source context
  add_page_type_pattern(pattern, page_type, notes='')
      teach classify_page() a new pattern without a code change
  suggest_page_type(page_text)
      ask Gemini to propose a category for unrecognized page text
  list_all_tables()
      every table this pipeline creates, grouped by layer

-- Stage 2 — run individually --
  run_text_only_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      ci_headlines + national_retail_readout
  run_major_changes_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      major_offer_changes
  run_voice_plan_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      voice_plan_comparison (image tier)
  run_biz_internet_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      business_internet_comparison (image tier)
  run_prepaid_grid_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      prepaid_price_grid_detail
  run_accessory_grid_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      prepaid_accessory_price_grid (image tier) — watch/tablet/gateway/hotspot
  run_service_offers_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      postpaid_service_offers
  run_carrier_grid_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      postpaid_bts_offers + cable_mvno_offers + prepaid_brand_offers
  run_device_offers_extraction(run_id, report_date)
      device offers incl. business (image tier)

-- Stage 2 — run everything --
  run_all_stage2_extractions(run_id, report_date)
      all 8 extractors in sequence, with per-stage crash isolation

Key Highlights – Week Ending 7/3/25:
• Best Buy’s carrier-locked promotions with AT&T and Verizon both focused mainly on the
Samsung Galaxy S25 series, including the S25 Edge, as well as the iPhone 15 Pro and Pro
Max. Discounts reach up to $1,000 off with trade-in and new line, or $300 off (Galaxy S25
Ultra), $350 off (Galaxy S25 Edge), or $400 (Galaxy S24 Ultra) without the qualifiers. The
iPhone 15 Pro and Pro Max are offered at $100 off with both carriers.
• Best Buy’s unlocked promotions feature up to $400 off the Samsung Galaxy Z Fold6, $250 off
the iPhone 14, $220 off the Galaxy S25 Edge, and $200 off the Galaxy S25 Ultra or Razr+
2024. Other unlocked promotions include Motorola, Nokia, Blu, HMD, and Google.
•
Walmart’s two new promotions offer $20 off the Samsung Galaxy A15 5G or $16 off the
Motorola G Play 2024 with Straight Talk or Verizon Prepaid, respectively.

COMPETITIVE INTELLIGENCE HEADLINES July 3, 2025
Postpaid & Cable MVNO Key Highlights
1. AT&T
• Wireless Account Lock – AT&T introduced a new feature which adds an extra layer of security to accounts, Wireless Account Lock. The feature requires an
account to be unlocked to add new lines, upgrade phones or initiate a Number Transfer PIN.
• $.99 iPad and Apple Watch Promos End – AT&T ended it’s $.99 Apple iPad and Apple Watch deals which had been in-market since May 2. The deal allowed
customers adding or upgrading to an iPhone 16 series device the ability add a BTS line and pay only $.99 for select iPads and/or select Apple Watches
(after monthly credits), BTS service was required on the iPad and Watch lines.
2. Verizon
• Trade Promotion Updates – Verizon will still accept phones in Any Condition for trade-in, but the carrier has reinstituted trade tiers. Older phones are worth
less than new phones and the values are once again tied to the rate plan. Example, an iPhone 11 qualifies for $1,000 off with Unlimited Ultimate vs. $600
with Welcome; an iPhone X qualifies for $600 with Unlimited Ultimate vs. $360 off with Unlimited Welcome. Verizon last had trade tiers for Upgrades in
May of 2024 while trade tiers for New Lines had been absent since September 2023 (iPhone 15 launch).
• Dialing Back Q2 Offers – Verizon made numerous other changes on July 3 which mostly resulted in a pulling back of promotional offers.
•
Line discounts for new accounts, in-market since early-March, were expired ($10, 1-line, $15, 2-3 lines, $20, 4+ lines).
• The $300 new line gift card in-market since May 15 was expired.
• BTS bundles which offered select tablets and watches free with a smartphone purchase, new BTS AAL and BTS service plan were scaled back. The
iPad offer went from $500 savings to $320 savings while watch offers were curtailed significantly; some $500 savings offers went to $120.
3. Xfinity Mobile
• No news or updates
4. Spectrum Mobile
• Galaxy Promos Expired – Spectrum Mobile ended promotions for the Galaxy S24 and S25 series of devices some of which had been in-market since
March. Spectrum’s promotions were mild compared to other carriers, $200 - $300 off FRPs.
T-Mobile Confidential

================================================================================
PAGE 6  |  page_type: ci_headlines  |  strategy: text_only
================================================================================
COMPETITIVE INTELLIGENCE HEADLINES July 3, 2025
Prepaid & MVNO Key Highlights
1. Cricket Wireless
• iPhone 13 returns to $49 for Switchers: After reducing it to $29 for one week (6/23 – 6/30), Cricket returned the iPhone 13 to $49 for customers porting w/activation on $60 rate plan
• Galaxy A16 5G $19.99 for New Lines: Cricket reduced the A16 5G to $19 (was $59) for customers adding a new line (no port req.) with activation on the $60 rate plan (6/30 – TBD)
2. Boost Mobile
• Multi-Line Pricing added Online: Boost added multi-line pricing for new customers to its online site – offering the same discounted pricing that is available in stores. However, initial orders
are limited to three lines – although more lines can be added later. Pricing is valid with BYO or with promotional phone offers. With the discounts – pricing is as follows:
• Unlimited Plus: 1-line $50, 2-lines $80, 3-lines $110, 4-lines $140, 5-lines $170
• Unlimited Premium: 1-line $60; 2-lines $100, 3-lines $140, 4-lines $180, 5-lines $220
• Boost Plus Stores: As reported by Wave7 Research, Boost Mobile has begun converting select stores to “Boost Plus” locations that are intended to be “postpaid-centric.” The plan is to
reportedly open 100+ stores within the next year. Signage will focus on the Infinite Access plans as well as select prepaid offers. One recent store opening was posted on LinkedIn.
3. Total Wireless
• Activation Fees Return: Total Wireless is once again charging a $25 activation fee for in-store purchases – with a cap of $50 for activations of two or more lines (7/1/25)
4. Visible
•
EXPIRED: Plan discounts with price-locks – expired $5 off Visible valid for 1 year (5/28 – 6/30) – and $5 off Visible+ valid for 3 years – or $5 off Visible+ Pro valid for 5 years; with BYO or new
phone (4/30 – 6/30; price lock valid beginning 5/28)
5. mobileX
• Ambassador Program: Launched via website (6/26/25) – the Ambassador Program allows customers who recruit friends/provide referrals to earn a “10% lifetime commission” for every
dollar brought in and a one-time $5 bonus if those customers port their number. Earnings are based on successful activations with at least one month of completed service.
6. Tracfone
• Phone Offers: New phone offers include $149 iPhone 12 with 3-month $40 plan or higher – and free A14 5G with $30 plan (7/1 – 9/3). Also offered free with select plans or multi-month
plans include moto g play 2023, moto g power 5G 2023, and BLU View 5 Pro (7/1 – 7/31).
T-Mobile Confidential

Key Highlights – Week Ending 7/3/25:
• Best Buy’s carrier-locked promotions with AT&T and Verizon both focused mainly on the
Samsung Galaxy S25 series, including the S25 Edge, as well as the iPhone 15 Pro and Pro
Max. Discounts reach up to $1,000 off with trade-in and new line, or $300 off (Galaxy S25
Ultra), $350 off (Galaxy S25 Edge), or $400 (Galaxy S24 Ultra) without the qualifiers. The
iPhone 15 Pro and Pro Max are offered at $100 off with both carriers.
• Best Buy’s unlocked promotions feature up to $400 off the Samsung Galaxy Z Fold6, $250 off
the iPhone 14, $220 off the Galaxy S25 Edge, and $200 off the Galaxy S25 Ultra or Razr+
2024. Other unlocked promotions include Motorola, Nokia, Blu, HMD, and Google.
•
Walmart’s two new promotions offer $20 off the Samsung Galaxy A15 5G or $16 off the
Motorola G Play 2024 with Straight Talk or Verizon Prepaid, respectively.

COMPETITIVE INTELLIGENCE HEADLINES July 3, 2025
Postpaid & Cable MVNO Key Highlights
1. AT&T
• Wireless Account Lock – AT&T introduced a new feature which adds an extra layer of security to accounts, Wireless Account Lock. The feature requires an
account to be unlocked to add new lines, upgrade phones or initiate a Number Transfer PIN.
• $.99 iPad and Apple Watch Promos End – AT&T ended it’s $.99 Apple iPad and Apple Watch deals which had been in-market since May 2. The deal allowed
customers adding or upgrading to an iPhone 16 series device the ability add a BTS line and pay only $.99 for select iPads and/or select Apple Watches
(after monthly credits), BTS service was required on the iPad and Watch lines.
2. Verizon
• Trade Promotion Updates – Verizon will still accept phones in Any Condition for trade-in, but the carrier has reinstituted trade tiers. Older phones are worth
less than new phones and the values are once again tied to the rate plan. Example, an iPhone 11 qualifies for $1,000 off with Unlimited Ultimate vs. $600
with Welcome; an iPhone X qualifies for $600 with Unlimited Ultimate vs. $360 off with Unlimited Welcome. Verizon last had trade tiers for Upgrades in
May of 2024 while trade tiers for New Lines had been absent since September 2023 (iPhone 15 launch).
• Dialing Back Q2 Offers – Verizon made numerous other changes on July 3 which mostly resulted in a pulling back of promotional offers.
•
Line discounts for new accounts, in-market since early-March, were expired ($10, 1-line, $15, 2-3 lines, $20, 4+ lines).
• The $300 new line gift card in-market since May 15 was expired.
• BTS bundles which offered select tablets and watches free with a smartphone purchase, new BTS AAL and BTS service plan were scaled back. The
iPad offer went from $500 savings to $320 savings while watch offers were curtailed significantly; some $500 savings offers went to $120.
3. Xfinity Mobile
• No news or updates
4. Spectrum Mobile
• Galaxy Promos Expired – Spectrum Mobile ended promotions for the Galaxy S24 and S25 series of devices some of which had been in-market since
March. Spectrum’s promotions were mild compared to other carriers, $200 - $300 off FRPs.
T-Mobile Confidential

================================================================================
PAGE 6  |  page_type: ci_headlines  |  strategy: text_only
================================================================================
COMPETITIVE INTELLIGENCE HEADLINES July 3, 2025
Prepaid & MVNO Key Highlights
1. Cricket Wireless
• iPhone 13 returns to $49 for Switchers: After reducing it to $29 for one week (6/23 – 6/30), Cricket returned the iPhone 13 to $49 for customers porting w/activation on $60 rate plan
• Galaxy A16 5G $19.99 for New Lines: Cricket reduced the A16 5G to $19 (was $59) for customers adding a new line (no port req.) with activation on the $60 rate plan (6/30 – TBD)
2. Boost Mobile
• Multi-Line Pricing added Online: Boost added multi-line pricing for new customers to its online site – offering the same discounted pricing that is available in stores. However, initial orders
are limited to three lines – although more lines can be added later. Pricing is valid with BYO or with promotional phone offers. With the discounts – pricing is as follows:
• Unlimited Plus: 1-line $50, 2-lines $80, 3-lines $110, 4-lines $140, 5-lines $170
• Unlimited Premium: 1-line $60; 2-lines $100, 3-lines $140, 4-lines $180, 5-lines $220
• Boost Plus Stores: As reported by Wave7 Research, Boost Mobile has begun converting select stores to “Boost Plus” locations that are intended to be “postpaid-centric.” The plan is to
reportedly open 100+ stores within the next year. Signage will focus on the Infinite Access plans as well as select prepaid offers. One recent store opening was posted on LinkedIn.
3. Total Wireless
• Activation Fees Return: Total Wireless is once again charging a $25 activation fee for in-store purchases – with a cap of $50 for activations of two or more lines (7/1/25)
4. Visible
•
EXPIRED: Plan discounts with price-locks – expired $5 off Visible valid for 1 year (5/28 – 6/30) – and $5 off Visible+ valid for 3 years – or $5 off Visible+ Pro valid for 5 years; with BYO or new
phone (4/30 – 6/30; price lock valid beginning 5/28)
5. mobileX
• Ambassador Program: Launched via website (6/26/25) – the Ambassador Program allows customers who recruit friends/provide referrals to earn a “10% lifetime commission” for every
dollar brought in and a one-time $5 bonus if those customers port their number. Earnings are based on successful activations with at least one month of completed service.
6. Tracfone
• Phone Offers: New phone offers include $149 iPhone 12 with 3-month $40 plan or higher – and free A14 5G with $30 plan (7/1 – 9/3). Also offered free with select plans or multi-month
plans include moto g play 2023, moto g power 5G 2023, and BLU View 5 Pro (7/1 – 7/31).
T-Mobile Confidential

• Best Buy’s carrier-locked promotions with AT&T and Verizon both focused mainly on the
Samsung Galaxy S25 series, including the S25 Edge, as well as the iPhone 15 Pro and Pro
Max. Discounts reach up to $1,000 off with trade-in and new line, or $300 off (Galaxy S25
Ultra), $350 off (Galaxy S25 Edge), or $400 (Galaxy S24 Ultra) without the qualifiers. The
iPhone 15 Pro and Pro Max are offered at $100 off with both carriers.
• Best Buy’s unlocked promotions feature up to $400 off the Samsung Galaxy Z Fold6, $250 off
the iPhone 14, $220 off the Galaxy S25 Edge, and $200 off the Galaxy S25 Ultra or Razr+
2024. Other unlocked promotions include Motorola, Nokia, Blu, HMD, and Google.

Walmart’s two new promotions offer $20 off the Samsung Galaxy A15 5G or $16 off the
Motorola G Play 2024 with Straight Talk or Verizon Prepaid, respectively.
